#  Information for Attorneys
![Information for Attorneys](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_icons_attorneys.png)
![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_attorneys_heading.jpg)
  

Case Information
[Appellate and Supreme Court Opinions](https://courts.delaware.gov/opinions/)
[Supreme Court Oral Argument Videos](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/oralarguments/)  
Only recordings of non-confidential cases argued in the Delaware Supreme Court are available. On days when the Delaware Supreme Court is [in session](https://courts.delaware.gov/calendars/list.aspx?ag=supreme%20court%20&srt=number), oral arguments can be viewed live through [Vimeo](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/oralarguments.aspx). 
[Supreme Court Case Scheduling FAQs](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/faqs.aspx)
[Supreme Court Most Common Brief Deficiencies](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=95508)  
The most frequent reasons the Clerk’s Office issues deficiency notices for briefs. It is not a list of all Supreme Court Rule requirements for briefs, but should be consulted before filing any brief. 
[Filing in the Court of Chancery](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=184178)  
Court Of Chancery publishes [revised Supplemental Information Form](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=6248). 
[Court Calendars](https://courts.delaware.gov/calendars/)
[Civil Case Search](https://courts.delaware.gov/docket.aspx)  
Access civil case information online 24-hours a day for the Superior Court, Court of Common Pleas and Justice of the Peace Court. 
[Court Forms](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/)  
Find frequently used Court forms for all State Courts in Delaware. 
Continuing Education
[Commission on Continuing Legal Education](https://courts.delaware.gov/cle/)  
Administers legal education compliance for members of the Delaware State Bar. 
[Review CLE Transcripts](https://www.desclms.org/Security/SignIn.aspx)  
Attorneys may sign in to their Attorney profile through the Delaware Supreme Court Lawyer Management System (DSCLMS) to review their CLE transcripts.
[Vincent A. Bifferato Trial Practice Forum](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/trialpracticeforum/)  
The Bifferato Trial Practice Forum's goal is to provide free continuing legal education (CLE) credits to those who are just starting out and to offer young attorneys a chance to network with each other as well as with more experienced attorneys. 
[Office of the Child Advocate CLE Trainings](https://courts.delaware.gov/childadvocate/attorneys/)  
The Office of the Child Advocate is now providing Web-based Continuing Legal Education and Professional Trainings online in addition to the traditional onsite continuing education opportunities. 
Attorney Ethics & Discipline
[Office Of Disciplinary Counsel](https://courts.delaware.gov/odc/)  
Regulates the practice of law by evaluating, investigating and prosecuting lawyer misconduct for the Court. 
[Attorney Disciplinary Decisions](https://courts.delaware.gov/odc/digest/)  
A database of disciplinary decisions. 
[Delaware Lawyers Rules of Professional Conduct](https://courts.delaware.gov/rules/)  

[Delaware Judges Code of Judicial Conduct](https://courts.delaware.gov/rules/)  

[Judicial Ethics Advisory Committee (JEAC)](https://courts.delaware.gov/jeac/)  
Opinions issued pursuant to Delaware Court on the Judiciary Rule 18 and to the rules of the Delaware Judicial Ethics Advisory Committee. 
[Court on the Judiciary](https://courts.delaware.gov/coj/)  
Considers ethical complaints against Delaware Judges. 
Opportunities to Serve
[Supreme Court Boards, Commissions and Committees](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/committees.aspx)  

[Office of the Child Advocate Volunteer Child Attorneys](https://courts.delaware.gov/childadvocate/attorneys/index.aspx)  

Courthouse Information
[Wireless Service in Courthouses](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=103848)  
The use of wireless networking throughout the courthouse allows attorney's to make use of wireless connectivity within the courthouse to connect to their office via the Internet without the need for a physical network connection. 
[Courtroom Equipment and Technology](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/courtroomtechnology.aspx)  
Information regarding the equipment and technology available for use by counsel in the Courtrooms throughout the State of Delaware. 
[Leonard L. Williams Justice Center](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/llwjc/)  
Learn about the policies, amenities, courtroom, evidence presentation equipment, and hours of operation for the Courthouse. 
[LLWJC Conference Room Request Form](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/roomrequest.aspx)  
Reserve a conference room in the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center for court-related business. 
[Facility Dog Request Form](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/facilitydog.aspx)  
Request the services of Officer Vinn, our courthouse facility dog. Vinn and his handler help families by easing stress for adults and children alike during legal proceedings. 
[Court of Chancery Conference Rooms](https://courts.delaware.gov/chancery/roomrequest.aspx)  
Conference rooms are available to court-related businesses (i.e. law firms, mediators, arbitrators) and those conducting business in the courthouse. 
[Kent County Courthouse](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/kccourthouse/)  
Learn about the policies, wireless access, evidence presentation equipment, and hours of operation for the Courthouse. 
[Sussex County Courthouse](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/sccourthouse/)  
Learn about the policies, evidence presentation equipment, and hours of operation for the Courthouse. 
[Judicial Law Libraries](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/)
[How to Request Interpreter Services](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/courtinterpreter/)
  

Attorney Information
[OCA Pro Bono Attorney/GAL](https://courts.delaware.gov/childadvocate/attorneys/)  
If you are an attorney licensed to practice law in the State of Delaware, you are eligible to represent an abused and/or neglected child through the Office of the Child Advocate. 
[Delaware Appellate Handbook](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=39398)  
The Delaware Appellate Handbook was prepared to assist Delaware attorneys in appellate practice before the Delaware Supreme Court, Court of Chancery, Superior Court and Family Court. 
[Annual Registration (DESCLMS)](https://www.desclms.org/Security/SignIn.aspx)  
Allows Delaware Attorneys to register and update lawyer profile information electronically. 
[Court Rules](https://courts.delaware.gov/rules/)  
Rules of the Delaware State Courts 
**Request a Bar Card**  
Please contact the Clerk’s office at (302) 739-4155 or email Lisa Dolph. Additionally, to obtain a new bar card, please contact the Delaware Lawyer Management System help desk at (302) 798-7500 or email helpdesk_desclms@doelegal.com. 
**Request a Certificate of Good Standing**   
Login to the [Delaware Supreme Court Lawyer Management System](https://www.desclms.org/Security/SignIn.aspx) to submit a request. 
Operating Procedures
[Operating Procedures for the Judicial Branch](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/operating-procedures/)
[Operating Procedures for the Supreme Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=117538)
[Operating Procedures for the Court of Chancery](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=84198)
[Administrative Directives for Superior Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/governance.aspx#directives)
[Administrative Directives for Court of Common Pleas](https://courts.delaware.gov/commonpleas/admdir.aspx)
[Policy Directives for Justice of the Peace Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/policy%20directives/)
Becoming a Lawyer
To practice law in Delaware, one must be licensed to do so. In order to be licensed one must submit an application, pass the Delaware Bar Exam and fulfill all of the prerequisites for admission to the Delaware Bar. Each year approximately 200 law school graduates apply to take the Delaware Bar Exam. There are currently more than 4,200 attorneys licensed in Delaware
[Board of Bar Examiners](https://courts.delaware.gov/bbe/)  
Considers applications for admission and results of examinations for admissions to the Delaware State Bar. 
[Overview of the Delaware Court System](https://courts.delaware.gov/overview.aspx)  
Learn about the Delaware Judiciary which is composed of the Supreme Court, the Court of Chancery, the Superior Court, the Family Court, the Court of Common Pleas, the Justice of the Peace Court, and related judicial agencies. 
**Clerkship and Internship Opportunities:**  

  * [Judicial Clerkships at the Supreme Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=87398)

#  Information for The Public
![Information for The Public](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_icons_public.png)
![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_public_heading.jpg)  

**TRAFFIC ALERT - Road closures and construction delays at and around the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington - Fall 2024 to June 2026.[Latest details on road closures.](https://courts.delaware.gov/traffic.aspx)**
## General Court Information
**Cellular telephones and other personal electronic devices are allowed in court facilities with restrictions which can be found in the[Portable Electronic Devices policy (PDF)](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=254158)**.
[Court Locations & Hours of Operation](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/)
[Court Contacts](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/contacts.aspx)
[Leonard L. Williams Justice Center](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/llwjc/)

[Sussex County Courthouse](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/sccourthouse/)

[Feedback](https://courts.delaware.gov/feedback/)
[Judicial Branch Operating Procedures](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/operating-procedures/)
[Overview of the Delaware Court System](https://courts.delaware.gov/overview.aspx)
## Helpful Videos
![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/A2J-video-explainer.jpg)
**Access to Justice Video Series**   
Informational videos to help understand complex legal processes and feel more confident navigating the court system. Closed captioning is available in multiple languages. The series includes videos on legal advice vs. legal information, navigating the court system without a laywer, understanding small claims court, demystifying legal procedures, and decoding court jargon. [Watch the entire Access to Justice Video Series.](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/videoseries.aspx)
**Civil Case Process in the Delaware Courts Video Series**  
The [video series on Civil Case Process in the Delaware Courts](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/civilvideos.aspx) includes videos on the steps of a lawsuit; starting, responding to and preparing your case; tips; and hearing information. The video series is also available in Spanish, [Proceso civil en los juzgados de Delaware](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/civilvideos_spanish.aspx). 
**Delaware’s Legacy—Brown v Board of Education**  
The state of Delaware played a significant role in desegregating public schools in the 1950s, through several key court cases decided in the Delaware Court of Chancery. The [Brown v. Board of Education web page](https://courts.delaware.gov/brownvboard.aspx) is an educational resource that provides key insights and details on that legacy through videos and original case documents. 
**What Makes the Delaware Court of Chancery Unique**  
The Delaware Court of Chancery is widely recognized as the nation's preeminent forum for the determination of disputes involving the internal affairs of the thousands upon thousands of Delaware corporations and other business entities through which a vast amount of the world's commercial affairs is conducted. Its unique competence in and exposure to issues of business law are unmatched. [What Makes the Delaware Court of Chancery Unique (YouTube)](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=K90D4poyx2I) video explains more about what virtues make it one of the most influential courts in the world.

Pay criminal and traffic fees.

## Self Help
Please visit our [Self Help section](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/) for more information on court proceedings, legal assistance, and general information on starting, responding to and preparing your case.
[Ask a Law Librarian](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/chat.aspx)—Submit your question to a law librarian  
_Please note: The law librarians are not attorneys; therefore they cannot provide any legal advice._
[Legal Assistance](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/legalassistance.aspx)
Legal Research—For [legal research tips, please consult our guide](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/legalresearch.aspx). For further assistance, please contact one of the state’s law libraries. Contact information, locations, and hours for the law libraries can be found on the [Judicial Law Libraries website](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/). You can also ask questions online by using our [Ask a Law Librarian service](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/chat.aspx).
[General FAQs](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/general-faqs.aspx)—Answers to frequently asked questions. 
Legal Glossaries:
  * [Supreme Court Citizens Guide](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/appeals/supremecitizensguide.aspx)
  * [Superior Court Legal Words Defined](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/superior_glossary.aspx)

#  Information for Jurors
![Information for Jurors](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_icons_jurors.png)
![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_juror_heading.jpg)   

**TRAFFIC ALERT - Road closures and construction delays at and around the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington - Fall 2024 to June 2026.[Latest details on road closures.](https://courts.delaware.gov/traffic.aspx)**   

  

## I've Been Summoned for Jury Duty: What Does That Mean?
You may be wondering what to expect when you are summoned for jury duty. Listed within the Jury Service website are juror tips and information about your jury service, including a description of the process by which you were selected, the real importance of a summons, a few reminders for your first day of jury service, security information, where to find your jury room, and what happens when you report for jury duty.
[Jury Service - The Basics](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_basics.aspx)
[Online Questionnaire for those Summoned for Jury Duty](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_form.aspx)
[Jury Reporting Instructions](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_reporting.aspx)
[Jury Service - About the Juror Summons](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_basics.aspx#summons)
[I Need a Postponement/ Want to Seek a Recusal](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_form_recusal.aspx)
[Frequently Asked Juror Questions](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_faq.aspx)
### Where Do I Go?
  

[Directions and Maps](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_maps.aspx)
[Parking Information](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_parking.aspx)
### What Do I Do When I Get to the Courthouse?
  

[Courthouse Security - What to Expect](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_security.aspx)
[Where is the Jury Room located in the Courthouse?](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_reporting.aspx)
### General Information
  

[About Jury Services](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_services.aspx)
[A Message from the Presiding Judge](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_message.aspx)

#  Delaware Courts
## Welcome to the Delaware Courts
Delaware's [court system](https://courts.delaware.gov/overview.aspx) is composed of the [Supreme Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/), [Court of Chancery](https://courts.delaware.gov/chancery/), [Superior Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/), [Family Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/family/), [Court of Common Pleas](https://courts.delaware.gov/commonpleas/), [Justice of the Peace Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/jpcourt/), [Administrative Office of the Courts](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/), and [related agencies](https://courts.delaware.gov/agencies.aspx). Read our [mission and vision statements](https://courts.delaware.gov/overview.aspx).
  
  

## Information For:
### [ _![Information for the Public](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_icons_public.png)_ The Public ](https://courts.delaware.gov/information_public.aspx)
### [ _![Information for Jurors](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_icons_jurors.png)_ Jurors ](https://courts.delaware.gov/information_jurors.aspx)
### [ _![Information for Attorneys](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_icons_attorneys.png)_ Attorneys ](https://courts.delaware.gov/information_attorneys.aspx)
### [ _![Information for the Media](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/info_icons_media.png)_ The Media ](https://courts.delaware.gov/information_media.aspx)
## Court Alerts
  *   
Bogus phone calls are on the rise, making false claims about warrants, jury duty, fines and fees and fraudulently demanding immediate payment. **[Learn more about phone scam warning](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=315938)**.
  *   
Road closures and construction delays at and around the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington - Fall 2024 to June 2026. [**Latest details on road closures.**](https://courts.delaware.gov/traffic.aspx)

## Helpful Services
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_hours.png)_ Hours & Locations ](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/)
Addresses and times for all courts by county. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_jury.png)_ Jury Instructions ](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_reporting.aspx)
Information on hours, pay, selection, etc. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_interpret.png)_ Court Interpreter Program ](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/courtinterpreter/)
How to become or request a Court interpreter. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_tickets.png)_ Pay Traffic Tickets ](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/traffic/)
Steps on how to pay a traffic ticket in Delaware. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_efiling.png)_ e-Filing System ](https://courts.delaware.gov/efiling/)
Learn how to eFile in the Delaware Court system. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_epayments.png)_ e-Payment System ](https://courts.delaware.gov/epayment.aspx)
Pay fines using your credit card. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_ada.png) _ Accessibility  ](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/ada.aspx)
Request accommodation for our court facilities. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_casesearch.png) _ Civil Case Search  ](https://courts.delaware.gov/docket.aspx)
Get access to our civil case online database. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_careers.png) _Careers & Employment  ](https://courts.delaware.gov/career/)
Start a career in the Delaware judicial branch. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_reports.png) _ Reports & Publications  ](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/publications.aspx)
Reports, publications and statistics of the Judiciary. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_tradenames.png) _ Trade Names ](https://revenue.delaware.gov/trade-business-and-fictitious-names-search/)
Research and register trade, business or fictitious names. 
### [ _![](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/services_icon_lawlib.png) _ Ask a Law Librarian  ](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/chat.aspx)
Submit your question to a law librarian.

#  Formularios y folletos en español
(Brochures and forms in Spanish)    

Para más información acerca de cómo ser un/a intérprete Judicial en Delaware, diríjase a [esta página](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/courtinterpreter/faqs.aspx).
## Instrucciones para solicitar intérprete — How to request interpreter services
  * [Instrucciones para solicitar intérprete](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=132938) (How to request interpreter services)


## Instrucciones para audiencias remotas por teléfono y video — Instructions for remote hearings via telephone and video
  * [Audiencias judiciales por ZOOM con un intérprete/Instrucciones para litigantes en español](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=125198) (Zoom Hearing/Interpreter Function Reference Guide SPANISH for LEP)
  * [Comuníquese con el Tribunal de Familia para proporcionar sus datos para una audiencia remota](https://courts.delaware.gov/family/remotehearingespanol.aspx) (Contact Information for Remote Hearing Submission)
  * [Zoom—información e instrucciones](https://courts.delaware.gov/family/zoom.aspx#spanish) (Zoom instructions and materials - Family Court)
  * [Presentación Civil por Correo Electrónico Tribunal de Familia del Estado de Delaware](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=123268) (Civil Filing by Email in the Family Court of Delaware)


## Proceso Judicial de Delaware — Delaware Judicial Process
  * [Tradición de excelencia](https://courts.delaware.gov/docs/TribunalDeJusticia.pdf) (Tradition of Excellence)
  * [Información para Litigantes en el Juzgado de Paz—Calendarios para personas que hablan español y criollo haitiano—El proceso con intérpretes](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/courtinterpreter/arraignment-process.aspx) (Spanish and Haitian-Creole Language Arraignment Calendars in the Justice of the Peace Court—Process with Interpreters)
  * [Proceso Civil en los Tribunales de Delaware](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/civilvideos_spanish.aspx)(Video series on civil case process in the Delaware Courts)
  * [Lectura formal y respuesta a los cargos](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=102328) (What is an Arraignment?)
  * [Cómo prepararse para su audiencia](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=159588) (Preparing for Your Hearing in Family Court)
  * [Información para litigantes y acusados](https://courts.delaware.gov/CommonPleas/docs/CCPProSepacketCrimSPANISH.pdf) (Court of Common Pleas Pro Se Packet)
  * [Protegiendo al cliente inocente- Fondo de abogados para la protección del cliente](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=84268)(Protecting the Innocent Legal Client)
  * [Declaración de la Querella](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=32838)/[(Word version)](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=32848) (Claim Form)
  * [Los Siguientes Pasos en su Caso Penal – adulto](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=110318)(Next Steps in a Delinquency or Criminal Matter in Family Court)
  * [Los Siguientes Pasos en su Caso Penal – juvenil](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=110328)(Next Steps in a Delinquency or Criminal Matter in Family Court)
  * [ Casos penales en el Tribunal de Familia](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/proceedings/fc_criminal-spanish.aspx) (Criminal Cases in the Family Court)
  * [Como presentar y defender una demanda civil en el Juzgado de Paz](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=110328)(How to File and Defend a Civil Claim - JP form BK04)
  * [Proceso para tramitar y disputar una demanda de desalojo por via sumaria en el Juzgado de Paz ](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=123458)(How to File and Defend a Summary Possession Action - JP form BK01)
  * [Preguntas y respuestas sobre la normativa probatoria en el Juzgado de Paz](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=123668)(Questions and Answers About the Rules of Evidence - JP form BK03)
  * [Aviso a todos los acusados que no pagan lo ordenado en su totalidad el dia de hoy](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=104398)(TTP Information Sheet - JP form GJ7141)
  * [Lo que necesita saber ante de venir al Juzgado de Paz](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=122408)(Visiting the Justice of the Peace Court- What you Need to Know - JP form GJ718V)
  * [Información para acusados en los Juzgados de Paz](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=266648)(Information for Defendants, JP Court)
  * [Asistencia Legal](https://courts.delaware.gov/help/legalassistance-spanish.aspx) (Legal Assistance)


## Proteccion por Abuso — Protection From Abuse
  * Llame al Programa de Ayuda a las Víctimas de Violencia Domestica (DVPA, por sus siglas en inglés) al 302-255-2609 si necesita ayuda para solicitar protección por abuso al juzgado. [Para información adicional](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=120738).
  * [Proteccion por Abuso Paquete de instrucciones](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=105228) (Protection From Abuse Instruction Packet)
  * [Proteccion por Abuso Preguntas frecuentes](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=105238) (Protection From Abuse FAQs)
  * [La audiencia de protección por abuso: lo que puede anticipar (El proceso paso a paso)](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=125918) (The PFA Hearing: What You Can Expect)


## Formularios de quejas — Complaint Forms Against an Employee
  * [Formulario de Quejas del Program de la Oficina Administrativa Judicial o AOC por sus siglas en inglés](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=126758) (AOC Complaint Form English/Spanish)
  * [Formulario de Quejas del Program de Intérpretes Judiciales o CIP, por sus siglas en inglés](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=238208) (Court Interpreter Program Complaint Form English/Spanish) 
  * [Procedimiento y formulario de quejas bilingüe inglés/español](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=51678) (Superior Court Complaint Policy and Procedure)
  * [Formulario de quejas](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=59848) (Justice of the Peace Court Complaint Form)
  * [Política de queja](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=51678) (Superior Court Complaint Policy Against an Employee)


## Multas y DUI — Traffic Tickets and DUI
  * [Como pagar o disputar una multa](http://deljis.delaware.gov/pdfs/SpanishInstructions.pdf) (Paying a traffic ticket, JP Court) 
  * [Preguntas frecuentes sobre tránsito, Juzgado de Paz](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=266628) (Frequently asked questions about traffic, JP Court)
  * [Delaware DUI descripción e instrucciones](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=59788) (Delaware DUI Evaluation/Referral Program Instructions, JP Court)

#  Ask A Law Librarian
Please complete and submit the following form:
Name (optional):   
Email Address (required):
@
  
County for the case (optional): None New Castle County Kent County Sussex County   
Court for the case (optional): None Supreme Court Court of Chancery Superior Court Family Court Court of Common Pleas Justice of the Peace Court   
Question (required):   

The law librarians are not attorneys; therefore they cannot provide any legal advice. Questions will be answered in the order they are received and it may take up to 72 hours for a response.
  

Submit
* * *
[New Castle Law Library](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/newcastle.aspx) | [Kent Law Library](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/kent.aspx) | [Sussex Law Library](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/sussex.aspx)
  

  
![Judicial Law Libraries](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/img/lawlibraries_inner_menu.jpg)
* * *
  * [Law Libraries Home](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/index.aspx)
  * [New Castle County](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/newcastle.aspx)
  * [Kent County](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/kent.aspx)
  * [Sussex County](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/sussex.aspx)

  * [Catalog](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/catalog.aspx)

##  Court of Common Pleas - Kent County
  

![Kent County Courthouse](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/img/2011_kent_crt_md.jpg)
  

**Address:**  
Kent County Courthouse  
414 Federal Street  
Dover, DE 19901 
**Hours:** Monday-Friday 8:30am - 4:30pm
**Phone Number:** [302-735-3900](tel:+13027353900)
**Parking** :
A courthouse parking lot is located on the north side of Water Street between State Street and Governor's Avenue. It is conveniently located within walking distance of the Kent County Courthouse.
* * *
**Helpful Links** :
  * [Court of Common Pleas home page](https://courts.delaware.gov/commonpleas/)
  * [Court Holidays/Closings](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/holidays.aspx)
  * [Kent County Courthouse](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/kccourthouse/)
  * [Courthouse Screening Policy](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=81028)
  * [DART Schedule](http://www.dartfirststate.com/routes/)


**Map**
Court of Common Pleas is located in the Kent County Courthouse at 414 Federal Street in Dover across the street from the Jesse Cooper Building.

##  Delaware State Courts - Holiday Schedule
  

### 2026 Holidays
24-hour Justice of the Peace Courts are not subject to State closings or holidays. 
Holiday
Date
Day
New Year's Day
January 1
Thursday
Martin Luther King Jr. Day
January 19
Monday
Good Friday
April 3
Friday
Memorial Day
May 25
Monday
Juneteenth
June 19
Friday
Independence Day
July 3
Friday
Labor Day
September 7
Monday
Election Day
November 3
Tuesday
Return Day
November 5 - after 12 noon for State employees  
living and/or working in Sussex County
Thursday
Veterans Day
November 11
Wednesday
Thanksgiving Day
November 26
Thursday
Day After Thanksgiving
November 27
Friday
Christmas Day
December 25

#  Hours & Locations

  * [Leonard L. Williams Justice Center](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/llwjc/)
  * [Kent County Courthouse](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/kccourthouse/)
  * [Sussex County Courthouse](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/sccourthouse/)
  * [Court Contacts](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/contacts.aspx)


  

##  Superior Court - New Castle County
  

**TRAFFIC ALERT - Road closures and construction delays at and around the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington - Fall 2024 to June 2026.  
[Latest details on road closures.](https://courts.delaware.gov/traffic.aspx)**
  

![Leonard L. Williams Justice Centere - New Castle County](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/img/sl_nc4.jpg)
  

**Address:**  
Leonard L. Williams Justice Center  
500 North King Street  
Wilmington, DE 19801 
**Hours:** Monday-Friday 8:30am - 4:30pm
**Phone Number:** [302-255-0800](tel:+13022550800)
* * *
**Jury Services Office (1st Floor):**
**Phone Number:** [302-255-0824](tel:+13022550824)
**Fax Number:** 302-255-2263
Court Administration, Suite 2850 - Level 2
Bailiffs, Suite 2609 - Level 2
Chambers, Suite 10400 - Level 10
Court Reporters, Suite 2609 - Level 2
Investigative Services, Suite 10 - Lower Level 2 (L2)
Judgments, Suite 1500 (Prothonotary) - Level 1
Jury Services, Suite 1800 - Level 1
Prothonotary, Suite 500 - Lower Level 1 (L1)
* * *
**Parking** :
The Leonard L. Williams Justice Center parking garage is attached to the courthouse. You must be prepared to pay for your own parking each day of your jury service. If you park in the garage attached to the Courthouse, be aware that the rate is $11 per day.
Superior Court does have limited number of free parking spaces in the garage attached to the Courthouse. However, no one is guaranteed free parking while on jury duty. If you leave before completing your service, you are not eligible for free parking. If you park in any parking facility other than the one attached to the Courthouse, the Court cannot pay for your parking.
Remember, you must be prepared to pay for your own parking each day regardless of where you park. The Court cannot guarantee free parking for any juror.
Additional parking is available to members of the public when the Courthouse Parking Garage is full. View a [list of parking garages](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/llwjc/parking.aspx) in close proximity to the courthouse. 
* * *
**Helpful Links** :
  * [Superior Court Home Page](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/)
  * [Court Holidays/Closings](https://courts.delaware.gov/locations/holidays.aspx)
  * [Leonard L. Williams Justice Center](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/llwjc/)
  * [Courthouse Screening Policy](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=81028)
  * [DART Schedule](http://www.dartfirststate.com/routes/)


**Map**
Superior Court is located at 500 N. King Street in the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in the City of Wilmington.

  2. Overview of the Courts


#  An Overview of the Delaware Court System
  

The Delaware Judiciary is composed of the Supreme Court, the Court of Chancery, the Superior Court, the Family Court, the Court of Common Pleas, the Justice of the Peace Court, and related judicial agencies.
In terms of interrelationships among the courts, the Delaware Court system is similar to a pyramid. The Justice of the Peace Court represents the base of the pyramid and the Supreme Court the apex of the pyramid. As a litigant goes upward through the court system pyramid, the legal issues generally become more complex and, thus, more costly to litigate.
  

## Mission Statement
* * *
To provide access to fair and effective justice in a safe and transparent environment through a diverse, inclusive, and dedicated workforce.
  

## Vision Statement
* * *
Equal justice through transparency, integrity, innovation, and judicial branch independence.
  

## Delaware Courts
* * *
The [Justice of the Peace Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/jpcourt/), the initial entry level into the court system for most citizens, has jurisdiction over civil cases in which the disputed amount is less than $25,000. In criminal cases, the Justice of the Peace Court hears certain misdemeanors and most motor vehicle cases (excluding felonies) and the Justices of the Peace may act as committing magistrates for all crimes. All permissible appeals are to the Court of Common Pleas, with the exception of findings of juvenile delinquency for contempt of court related to truancy proceedings which may be appealed to Family Court. The Justice of the Peace Court is authorized by the Constitution of Delaware, Article IV, Section 1.
The [Court of Common Pleas](https://courts.delaware.gov/commonpleas/) has jurisdiction in civil cases where the amount in controversy, exclusive of interest, does not exceed $75,000 (as of October 21, 2019). In criminal cases, the Court of Common Pleas handles all misdemeanors occurring in the State except certain drug-related offenses and traffic offenses. Appeals may be taken to the Superior Court. The Court is also responsible for all preliminary hearings in felony cases. The statewide Court of Common Pleas was created by Title 10, Chapter 13 of the Delaware Code, effective July 5, 1973. By Act of the General Assembly on April 26, 2005, the Court of Common Pleas became a Constitutional Court, pursuant to Article IV, Section 7B of the Delaware Constitution.
The [Family Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/family/) has extensive jurisdiction over virtually all family and juvenile matters. All civil appeals, including those relating to juvenile delinquency, go directly to the Supreme Court while criminal cases are appealed to the Superior Court. The Constitution of Delaware, Article IV, Section 1, authorizes the Family Court.
The [Superior Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/), the State's court of general jurisdiction, has original jurisdiction over criminal and civil cases except equity cases. The Court has exclusive jurisdiction over felonies and almost all drug offenses. In civil matters, the Court's authority to award damages is not subject to a monetary maximum. The Superior Court also serves as an intermediate appellate court by hearing appeals on the record from the Court of Common Pleas, the Family Court (in criminal cases), and a number of administrative agencies. Appeals from the Superior Court may be taken to the Supreme Court.
The [Court of Chancery](https://courts.delaware.gov/chancery/) has jurisdiction to hear all matters relating to equity. The litigation in this tribunal deals largely with corporate issues, trusts, estates, other fiduciary matters, disputes involving the purchase of land and questions of title to real estate as well as commercial and contractual matters. The Court of Chancery has a national reputation in the business community and is responsible for developing the case law in Delaware on corporate matters. Appeals from the Court of Chancery may be taken to the Supreme Court.
The [Supreme Court](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/) is the State's appellate court which receives direct appeals from the Court of Chancery, the Superior Court, and the Family Court. As administrative head of the courts, the Chief Justice of the Supreme Court, in consultation with the other justices, sets administrative policy for the court system. The Supreme Court is created by the Constitution of Delaware, Article IV, Section 1. The Supreme Court sits in Dover but the justices maintain their chambers in the counties where they reside.
  

## Administrative Office of the Courts
* * *
[The Administrative Office of the Courts](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/), including the [Judicial Information Center](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/jic.aspx), the [Office of the State Court Collections Enforcement](https://courts.delaware.gov/aoc/oscce/), and the [Law Libraries](https://courts.delaware.gov/lawlibraries/), provides those centralized services to the Delaware judiciary which are consistent with the statewide policies and goals for judicial administration and support operations as established by the chief justice of the Supreme Court.
  

## Arms of the Supreme Court
* * *
The [Board of Bar Examiners](https://courts.delaware.gov/bbe/) has the duties and powers set forth in Supreme Court Rule 51. The Board considers written applications for admission and the results of the examinations for admissions to the Delaware State Bar.
[Commission on Continuing Legal Education](https://courts.delaware.gov/cle/): Minimum Continuing Legal Education requirements for members of the Delaware Bar were established by the Supreme Court to ensure that attorneys and members of the judiciary maintain their professional competence. The Commission on Continuing Legal Education administers this rule by approving courses and activities and monitoring compliance with the mandate.
The [Lawyer's Fund for Client Protection (LFCP)](https://courts.delaware.gov/lfcp/) is a fund created by the Delaware Supreme Court to provide monetary relief to clients who have suffered financial losses as a result of the dishonest conduct of lawyers. While acts of attorney dishonesty are the exceptions and not the rule, the Fund was established to show the good faith of all the members of the Delaware Bar.
The[ Office of Disciplinary Counsel (ODC)](https://courts.delaware.gov/odc/) assists the Court in regulating the practice of law. In this capacity, the ODC is charged with evaluating, investigating, and, if warranted, prosecuting lawyer misconduct.
  

## Non-Judicial Agencies in the Judicial Branch Budget
* * *
Other agencies associated with the Delaware Judiciary include the state funded agencies: [Delaware Residents' Protection Commission](https://courts.delaware.gov/drpc/), [Maternal and Child Death Review Commission](https://courts.delaware.gov/childdeath/), [Office of the Child Advocate](https://courts.delaware.gov/childadvocate/), and [Public Guardian](https://courts.delaware.gov/publicguardian/). The majority of the components of the Delaware judicial system are funded by the State. Exceptions to this are the Registers of Wills for the Court of Chancery and the Sheriff's Offices. [Find more information about these non-judicial agencies.](https://courts.delaware.gov/agencies.aspx)

##  Juror Reporting Information
  

**NOTICE: Courthouse Entry**
Leonard L. Williams Justice Center opens for Jurors at 8:00am.  
Kent County Courthouse opens for Jurors at 8:15am.  
Sussex County Court house opens for Jurors at 8:30am. 
**only** report when you are needed.
**Daily Juror Reporting Information Online**
The Daily Juror Reporting Instructions are posted online after 6:00 p.m. for jurors reporting the next day. You may click the county you are to report for your Jury Service and obtain the latest update for the next day.
[New Castle County](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_reporting_modal_content.aspx?county=New+Castle)
  

[Kent County](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_reporting_modal_content.aspx?county=Kent)
  

[Sussex County](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/jury_reporting_modal_content.aspx?county=Sussex)
  
  
  

**Daily Juror Reporting Information by Phone**
****New Castle County****  
  
After 6:00pm the night before you are scheduled to report, you may call the **Jury Information Line at the following numbers depending on the panel for which you were summoned** : 
**Petit Jury** , after 6:00pm, the night before you are scheduled to report for jury duty, please **call[(302) 255-2491](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3022552491)**. 
**Grand Jury** , after 6:00pm, the night before you are scheduled to report for Grand Jury Duty, please **call[(302) 255-2547](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3022552547)**.
**Jurors selected for trial** should call, after 6:00pm, their Judge’s Information Line as distributed during Jury Selection for reporting instructions. 
* * *
****Kent County****  
  
Depending on the type of trial you have been summoned for will depend on what number you are to call. The Jury Type appears in the upper right-hand corner of your Summons. If you have been summoned for a:  

**Petit Jury** , after 6:00 p.m. the night before you are scheduled to report for jury duty, please **call[(302) 739-5328](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3027395328)**; or
**Special Jury** , after 6:00 p.m. the night before you are scheduled to report for jury duty, please **call[(302) 739-4666](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3027394666).**
You will hear a recording, which lists each group, by number, explaining when and where you are to report. (Your group number appears in the upper right-hand corner of your Summons above the Jury Type.)
* * *
****Sussex County****  
  
After 6:00 p.m. the night before you are scheduled to report, **call[(302) 856-5624](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3028565624)**
You will hear a recording which lists each group, by number, explaining when and where to report. Your Group Number and Jury Type appears in the upper right-hand corner of your Summons. 
* * *
**General Information for Juror Reporting**
_Juror Qualification Questionnaire_ with you if you did not email, mail, fax or submit it online to Superior Court Jury Services.
There are phones available for jurors to use in the Jury Assembly Room. 
In **New Castle County ONLY** , there are 40 lockers (at a cost of $1) for individuals to store their possessions in while they are inside the building. These lockers are located outside of the Courthouse, in the parking garage by the entrance. **If you choose not to use those lockers, please leave your items in your car or at home**.
Capitol Police will not allow any food, drinks or medications into the building. If you have a medical condition that requires these items accompany you into the Courthouse, please provide documentation (doctor’s note) upon entry.
**Where is the Jury Room Located in the Courthouse?**
**New Castle County**
![](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/agency/img/superior-ncc-courthouse.jpg)
**Leonard L. Williams Justice Center**
The Jury Assembly Room is on the 1st Floor of the Courthouse which is located at:
500 North King Street, Suite 1800  
Wilmington, DE 19801  
**[(302) 255-0800](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3022550800)**
The Leonard L. Williams Justice Center is open to the jurors and the public at 8:30 a.m.
After you enter the building, you will go through a security checkpoint and the metal detectors. Turn right after going through security. (Do not get on the escalators.) Go past the “Down Escalators” and continue walking until you reach the third set of doors on your left. This will be Jury Services. Please check in with the Jury Clerk at the desk. Be sure to bring your completed Qualification Questionnaire that is on the bottom part of your Juror Summons unless you have previously mailed, faxed or submitted this online. 
Please remember to bring your parking stub with you into the Courthouse. We validate the parking stubs inside of the Courthouse. Therefore, if you do not have your parking stub with you, we may not be able to validate it.
**Note** : In the event there is inclement weather, jurors must call 302-255-0555 before leaving your home or work for any late-breaking updates.
**Kent County**
![](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/agency/img/superior-kent-county-courthouse.jpg)
**Kent County Courthouse**
The Jury Assembly Room is on the 1st Floor of the Courthouse which is located at:
414 Federal Street  
Dover, DE 19901  
**[(302) 735-1900](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3027351900)** Ext. 58021 
The Kent County Courthouse opens to the jurors and the public at 8:15 a.m.
After passing through the security checkpoint, please proceed down the hallway past the stairs and turn right at the end of the hallway. The Jury Assembly Room is the last office on the left.
**Note** : In the event there is inclement weather, jurors must call **[(302) 739-5328](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3027395328)** for the most up-to-date information before leaving your home or work for any late-breaking updates.
**Sussex County**
![](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/agency/img/superior-sussex-county-courthouse.jpg)
**Sussex County Courthouse**
The Jury Assembly Room is on the 1st Floor of the Courthouse which is located at:
1 The Circle  
Georgetown, DE 19947  
**[(302) 855-7055](https://courts.delaware.gov/superior/jury/+tel:3028557055)**
The Sussex County Courthouse opens to the jurors and the public at 8:30am.
**Note** : In the event there is inclement weather, jurors must call the designated courthouse telephone before leaving your home or work for any late-breaking updates.

# Traffic Alert
## Road and lane closures due to construction around the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington
Starting in the Fall of 2024, those who regularly use N. King Street in the city of Wilmington or have business at the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center at 500 N. King Street, should be prepared to encounter traffic disruptions and traffic pattern changes. This includes one lane of N. King Street directly in front of the Custom House and on Alico Road, the road leading to the courthouse parking garage. The lane closures and changes are necessary due to the ongoing renovation and expansion of the historic Custom House property at 516 N. King Street.
**ACTIVE UPDATES ON ROAD CLOSURES**
* * *
October 28, 2025—[Alico Road at the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington closed until further notice](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=309878)  

* * *
September, 2025—[Closure of Alico Road extended to Nov. 3 at the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=306018)  

* * *
August 4, 2025—[Alico Road at Leonard L. Williams Justice Center to close on Monday Aug. 11, 2025 for six weeks](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=300038)  

* * *
[View all published updates](https://courts.delaware.gov/traffic.aspx#updates)
  

  
Legend
**Road and lane closures due to construction around the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center in Wilmington**
![yellow legend square with diagonal single lines](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/legend-yellow60.jpg)—IN YELLOW ON MAP—One lane of N. King Street in front of the Custom House closed starting on Nov. 18, 2024. It will remain closed for approximately 20 months during Custom House construction.  
  
![blue legend square with diagonal double lines](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/legend-blue60.jpg)—IN BLUE ON MAP—Alico Road from N. King Street to the Parking Garage will remain open but will be subject to periodic closures and being reduced to one lane during construction. Dates of closures and changes will be posted on this page.  
  
![red legend square with crossed lines](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/legend-red60.jpg)—IN RED ON MAP—This section of Alico Road closed on Nov. 14, 2024. 
During the construction, there will still be access to the courthouse parking garage – operated by Colonial Parking – from the Walnut Street side of the garage. (Using the address 537 North Walnut St. on a GPS device will bring you to the Walnut St. entrance.)
Drivers will also not be allowed to park or stand on Alico Road during construction or use Alico Road to drop off passengers at the courthouse. Traffic on the road and space limitation will prevent a U-turn back out onto N. King Street.
  
![Map of the area around the Custom House, next to the Leonard L. Williams Justice Center, that will be affected by construction and lane closures. From the bottom left, the map highlights one lane in yellow on N. King Street, directly in front of the custom house. Next, on the left side of the map, Alico Road that takes drivers from N. King Street to the parking garage is highlighted in blue. Finally, the map highlights the last part of Alico Road, from the parking garage back out to N. King Street in red.](https://courts.delaware.gov/img/TrafficPlan.jpg)

#  Terms of Use
  
[**Reglas de uso en español**](https://courts.delaware.gov/reglas.aspx)  

  

## Disclaimer
* * *
Thank you for visiting the Delaware Courts web site. The Judicial Branch of the State of Delaware makes every effort to ensure the dissemination of timely, accurate public information on this site, and provide it for your use and convenience. Although the information on the site is believed to be correct, its accuracy cannot be guaranteed. We revise and update our rules and schedules on a regular basis, and will update our website as quickly as possible to reflect changes, but delays may occur. The Judicial Branch shall not be held liable for any losses caused by reliance on the accuracy or reliability of this website.
  

## Translation Disclaimer
* * *
Translations are provided to assist limited English proficient persons. If there are differences between English and another language, the English version is the official version.
  

## Links to other sites
* * *
The site contains links to other sites. The Judicial Branch does not favor any one group over another, nor does the use of any link to any organization's web site herein constitute an endorsement of that organization. The Delaware Judicial Branch is not responsible for the contents, accuracy and privacy practices of those sites.
  

## Links from other sites
* * *
The Judicial Branch specifically disclaims any and all liability for damages which may result from the accessing of a third party site, which is linked to the Delaware Courts web site, or from reliance upon any, and such information.
**Information Collected at this site:**
When you visit this site, your web browser may automatically send some basic information to us. This information is used solely to help us make this site more useful to visitors, to learn about the number of visitors to our site, and the kinds of technology they use. All of this helps us ensure that this site is as useful as possible. Basic information that may be collected includes:
  * The Internet Protocol (IP) Address and domain name used. The IP Address is a numerical identifier assigned either to your Internet service provider or directly to your computer;
  * The type of browser and operating system you used;
  * The date and time you visited this site;
  * The web pages or services you accessed at this site;
  * The web site you visited prior to coming to this web site;
  * The web site you visit as you leave this web site; and
  * If you downloaded a form, the form that was downloaded.

  

## Cookies
* * *
**Use of Cookies** :
Visitors to the Delaware Courts site can access the Web site without accepting cookies.
**What is a Cookie?**  
There are two general types of cookies that web sites make use of:  
Session cookies — these are cookies created by a web site that exist only as long as your visit to that web site. They are not stored permanently on your computer.  
Persistent cookies — these cookies are stored on your computer by a web site for some period of time and are used when you return to that site in the future. 
**What exactly does a cookie do?**  
A cookie provides a way for a web site to keep track of a user's patterns and preferences. Cookies contain a range of web site addresses for which they are valid. When a user's web browser encounters those addresses again, it sends those specific cookies to the Web server. For example, if a user's specific preferences were stored as a cookie, it would save that person from typing in the same information all over again when accessing that service for the second and subsequent times. 
**What won't a cookie do?**  
Certain web-based applications may require users to establish an user ID and Password. A cookie that is stored on your computer for these applications will not incorporate these separate user ID's and passwords. Should a third party use your computer they will not have access to personal information (e.g., your name or e-mail address) simply by virtue of having cookies stored on your computer. If you do not want cookies stored on your computer, you should read carefully the information contained in the section entitled "What options do I have with respect to cookies?" 
**What options do I have with respect to cookies?**  
You can have your browser disable cookies or prompt you before accepting a cookie. Look for the cookie options in your browser in the "Options" or "Preferences" menu. 
  

## Security:
* * *
To protect the system from unauthorized use and to ensure that the system is functioning properly, system administrators monitor this system. Anyone using this system expressly consents to such monitoring and is advised that if such monitoring reveals possible conduct of criminal activity, system personnel may provide evidence of such monitoring to law enforcement officers.
  

## Email Management
* * *
You may choose to provide us with personal information, as in e-mail with a comment or question. This information is used to improve our service to you or to respond to your request. Sometimes we share your e-mail with other State employees who may be better able to help you, and this staff may be employed by a different agency within the State. By law, we cannot share this information with individuals (including state employees) that do not require it as a normal part of their official duties. Except for authorized law enforcement investigations or, as required by law, we do not share our e-mail with any other entities without your consent.
We use your e-mail to respond appropriately. This may be to respond to you, to email to another agency for appropriate action. Once the issue or concern that is raised via e-mail is resolved, this information will not be retained unless required by state law or agency regulation.
The Delaware Judicial Branch will not distribute your information to third parties for direct marketing or e-mail marketing purposes. The information collected at this site will remain confidential to the extent permitted by state and federal law.
  

## Copyright Notice
* * *
Use and/or display of the Seal of Delaware is limited by law, and requires written permission from the State of Delaware as authorized by the Secretary of State and the Governor.
All rights, including any copyright or other proprietary interest of the State of Delaware, in the information and material contained in this web site are reserved. The posting of information or material on the web site does not alter or relinquish any copyright or other proprietary interest of the State in it.
To obtain any required permission to reproduce or otherwise use information (text or graphic) contained on the Judiciary web site, submit the specifics of your request to the State Court Administrator.
  

## Privacy
* * *
It is the policy of the Judicial Branch to preserve the privacy of personal records and to protect confidential or privileged information obtained through the use of the web site.
The Privacy Policy does not cover personal or identifying information about litigants that may appear in published appellate court opinions posted on the Delaware Courts web site.

#  Access to Justice Commission
  

## Criminal Justice Improvement Commission
* * *
### Improved Criminal Code
[The Final Report to the Delaware General Assembly’s Criminal Justice Improvement Committee Vol.1 and Vol. 2](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/criminalcode.aspx)
## Supreme Court Justice Valihura and Family Court Chief Judge Newell promote _pro bono_ representation at American Bar Association Event
* * *
Justice Karen L. Valihura of the Delaware Supreme Court and Chief Judge Michael K. Newell of the Delaware Family Court promoted the virtues of representing indigent litigants to a meeting of the American Bar Association (ABA) held on Feb. 27, 2019 in Wilmington at the law offices of Young Conaway, Stargatt & Taylor. [Read more about pro bono representation at ABA event.](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=110808)
![Justice Valihura and Chief Judge Newell at American Bar Association Event](https://courts.delaware.gov/supreme/agency/img/ValihuraProBono.jpg)
## Access to Justice Pro Bono Challenge
* * *
The Pro Bono Challenge will begin on January 1, 2019 and run through December 31, 2019.
Participants are asked to commit to dedicating at least 1% of their professional hours for the 2019 calendar year to pro bono service to indigent individuals and families.
[The Delaware Access to Justice Commission Announces The Pro Bono Challenge.](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=107898)
  

## Access to Justice Civil Subcommittees Final Report
* * *
The Delaware Supreme Court created the Access to Justice Commission in 2014 “to identify the critical needs related to access to justice in Delaware and to develop realistic and cost effective solutions to meet those needs.” In order to accomplish that directive, three subcommittees focusing on civil justice were created: 
  * The Subcommittee on the Efficient Delivery and Adequate Funding of Legal Services to the Poor (the Funding Subcommittee);
  * The Subcommittee on Judicial Branch Coordination in Helping Pro Se Litigants (the Pro Se Subcommittee); and
  * The Subcommittee on Promoting Greater Private Sector Representation of Underserved Litigants (the Pro Bono Subcommittee).

On Sept. 18, 2017 the three civil Subcommittees completed their work and below is their Final Report to the Delaware Supreme Court. 
[Access to Justice Civil Subcommittees Final Report](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98738)
View/print report in sections: 
  * [Report Cover](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98688)
  * [Report Overview](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98698)
  * [Funding Subcommittee Report](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98708)
  * [Pro Se Subcommittee Report](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98718)  
[Pro Se Subcommittee Report Exhibits](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98768)
  * [Pro Bono Subcommittee Report ](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98728)   
[Pro Bono Subcommittee Report Exhibits](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=98878)

  

##  Disparity Study
* * *
Following through on recommendations issued by criminal justice experts from Bryan Stevenson’s Equal Justice Institute and the Quattrone Center for the Fair Administration of Justice during a series of public hearings on criminal justice reform in the fall of 2015, the Delaware Access to Justice Commission’s Committee on Fairness in the Criminal Justice System on Sept. 23, 2016 released an independent study that looks into the issue of racial disparities in the Delaware criminal justice system 
Press release: [Study on the role of race in the Delaware criminal justice system](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=89818)
Report: [Evaluating the Role of Race in Criminal Justice Adjudications in Delaware](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147168)
  

## Background
* * *
The Delaware Access to Justice Commission held its kickoff meeting on December 15, 2014 at the Arsht Hall University of Delaware, Wilmington, Delaware. The Commission has been established by the Delaware Supreme Court to undertake the task of examining the justice system to identify any barriers to access to justice that may exist, and to develop recommendations designed to improve access to justice for the citizens of Delaware. To increase its accountability, the voting membership of the Commission are comprised entirely of private citizens — outstanding community and business leaders, lawyers and other professionals from across the state, who have the flexibility to make whatever policy recommendations they believe will be best for Delaware.
The Commission, working through committees, will initially focus on four important access to justice needs in Delaware — the efficient delivery and adequate funding of legal services to the poor; Judicial Branch coordination in helping self-represented litigants; the need to increase the pool of legal advisors to help litigants of limited means by exploring roadblocks confronting those lawyers; and fairness in the adult criminal justice system. The Commission has been tasked with completing its initial work in two years, with various committees conducting research, holding public hearings and making recommendations throughout that time period. The Amended Order establishing the Access to Justice Commission and the Commission and subcommittee membership list can be found below.
Press Release: [Delaware Access to Justice Commission Gets Underway](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=81298)
[Amended Order establishing the Access to Justice Commission](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147178)
[Access to Justice Commission Members](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=83828)
  

**Committee Membership Lists:**  
[Efficient Delivery and Adequate Funding of Legal Services to the Poor](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=83788)  
[Judicial Branch Coordination in Helping Pro Se Litigants](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=83798)  
[Promoting Greater Private Sector Representation of Underserved Litigants](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=83808)  
[Fairness in the Criminal Justice System](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=83818)
  

## Access to Justice Public Hearings
* * *
The Access to Justice Commission's Committee on Fairness in the Criminal Justice System conducted a series of public hearings between October 22, 2015 and December 9, 2015. The Committee, comprised of prosecutors, defense attorneys, law enforcement, community leaders and academics, examined the causes of racial disparity in the criminal justice system and proposed ways to reduce those disparities.
Experts from the University of Pennsylvania Law School's Quattrone Center for the Fair Administration of Justice, Bryan Stevenson's Equal Justice Initiative, and the University of Delaware presented research on initiatives to reduce crime and increase racial equity.
  

## Access to Justice Committee Reports 2015
* * *
  * [A Report on Alternatives to Incarceration](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147188), Delaware Access to Justice Commission's Committee on Fairness in the Criminal Justice System — _prepared by the Equal Justice Initiative, October 2015_

  * [Understanding the Lived Experience of Dis-Opportunity](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147208), Access to Justice Commission Hearing: Education and Root Causes Committee — _Yasser Arafat Payne, Ph. D.,Associate Professor, Department of Black American Studies, University of Delaware_
  * [Justice Commission Report on Drugs and Health](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147218) — _Lana Harrison, Ph.D. Dept. of Sociology & Criminal Justice, University of Delaware_
  * [Unconscious Bias and the Criminal Justice System](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147228) — _Leland Ware, Louis L. Redding Professor University of Delaware. This presentation is derived from, A Comparative Analysis of Unconscious and Institutional Discrimination in the United States and Britain, 36 Ga. J. Int'l & Comp. L. 89 (2007)_

  * [A Report on the Root Causes of Racial Disparities in Delaware's Criminal Justice System](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147258), Delaware Access to Justice Commission's Committee on Fairness in the Criminal Justice System — _prepared by the Equal Justice Initiative, October 2015_
  * [Overview of Poverty in Delaware](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147268), _Center for Community Research & Service, October 2015_
  * [A Report on Bail & Pretrial Detention](https://courts.delaware.gov/forms/download.aspx?id=147278), Delaware's Access to Justice Commission's Committee on Fairness in the Criminal Justice System — _prepared by the Equal Justice Initiative, October 2015_
